```
     7→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/AST2CHIR.h"
     8→
     9→#include "cangjie/AST/Match.h"
    10→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
    11→#include "cangjie/Basic/Match.h"
    12→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/AST2CHIRChecker.h"

    14→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/GlobalDeclAnalysis.h"

    21→#include "cangjie/Utils/ConstantsUtils.h"
    22→#include "cangjie/Utils/ParallelUtil.h"

    24→namespace Cangjie::CHIR {
    25→bool AST2CHIR::HasFailed() const
    26→{
    27→    return this->failure;
    28→}
    29→
    30→void AST2CHIR::RegisterAllSources()
    31→{
    32→    auto& sources = sourceManager.GetSources();
    33→    for (auto idToSource : sources) {
    34→        auto& source = idToSource.second;
    35→        auto filePath = source.path;
    36→        auto absPath = FileUtil::GetAbsPath(source.path);
    37→        if (absPath.has_value()) {
    38→            filePath = absPath.value();
    39→        } else {
    40→            filePath = FileUtil::Normalize(filePath);
    41→        }
    42→        builder.GetChirContext().RegisterSourceFileName(source.fileID, filePath);
    43→    }
    44→}
    45→
    46→void AST2CHIR::CollectStaticInitFuncInfo()
    47→{
    48→    auto collectStaticInitFuncInfo = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& funcs) {
    49→        for (auto& func : funcs) {
    50→            if (!IsStaticInitializer(*func)) {
    51→                continue;
    52→            }
    53→            // Get all the static member variables which are inited by this `static.init` func
    54→            std::vector<Ptr<const AST::VarDecl>> staticVars;
    55→            Ptr<const AST::VarDecl> staticInitVar = nullptr;
    56→            auto parentDecl = StaticCast<const AST::InheritableDecl*>(func->outerDecl);
    57→            for (auto memberVar : GetStaticMemberVars(*parentDecl)) {
    58→                // Skip the generated class_static_init variable
    59→                if (memberVar->identifier == STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
    60→                    staticInitVar = memberVar;
    61→                    continue;
    62→                }
    63→                // Skip the variable which has default init value
    64→                if (memberVar->initializer != nullptr) {
    65→                    continue;
    66→                }
    67→                staticVars.emplace_back(memberVar);
    68→                varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.emplace(memberVar);
    69→            }
    70→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(func->outerDecl);
    71→            staticInitFuncInfoMap.emplace(
    72→                func->outerDecl, StaticInitInfo(StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(func), staticInitVar, staticVars));
    73→        }
    74→    };
    75→    collectStaticInitFuncInfo(globalAndMemberFuncs);
    76→}
    77→
    78→void AST2CHIR::CollectFuncsAndVars()
    79→{
    80→    auto collectVars = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& candidateVars) {
    81→        for (auto& var : candidateVars) {
    82→            // Skip the static variables which are inited by the `static init func`
    83→            if (var->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::STATIC) && var->identifier != STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
    84→                bool fromCommon = var->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::FROM_COMMON_PART);
    85→                bool initedInStaticInit = varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.find(var) != varsInitedByStaticInitFunc.end();
    86→                if (!fromCommon && initedInStaticInit) {
    87→                    continue;
    88→                }
    89→            }
    90→            funcsAndVars.AddElement(var);
    91→            fileAndVarMap[var->curFile].emplace_back(var);
    92→        }
    93→    };
    94→    collectVars(globalAndStaticVars);
    95→
    96→    auto collectFuncs = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& candidateFuncs) {
    97→        for (auto& func : candidateFuncs) {
    98→            if (func->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::MAIN_ENTRY) || func->identifier == MAIN_INVOKE) {
    99→                continue;
   100→            }
   101→            funcsAndVars.AddElement(func);
   102→        }
   103→    };
   104→    collectFuncs(globalAndMemberFuncs);
   105→}
   106→
   107→void AST2CHIR::CollectLocalConstFuncAndVars(const AST::Package& pkg)
   108→{
   109→    CollectLocalConstDecl collector;
   110→    collector.Collect(globalAndStaticVars, true);
   111→    collector.Collect(globalAndMemberFuncs, true);
   112→
   113→    /*  some const decl in member var can't be collected by visiting `init` func
   114→        class CA {
   115→            var b = { => const a = 1 }
   116→        }
   117→        member var `b` has default value, its default value doesn't show in CA.init func
   118→    */
   119→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> instanceMemberVars;
   120→    for (auto& decl : nominalDecls) {
   121→        for (auto member : decl->GetMemberDeclPtrs()) {
   122→            if (member->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL && !member->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::STATIC)) {
   123→                instanceMemberVars.emplace_back(member);
   124→            }
   125→        }
   126→    }
   127→    collector.Collect(instanceMemberVars, true);
   128→
   129→    /*  some local func decl can't be collected by visiting its outer decl
   130→        func foo() {
   131→            const func goo<T>() {}
   132→            goo<Int32>()
   133→        }
   134→        we can only collect goo's generic declare by visiting func foo, goo's instantiated declare can't be seen
   135→        goo's instantiated declare can only be seen in `pkg.genericInstantiatedDecls`
   136→    */
   137→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> instLocalconstFuncs;
   138→    for (auto& decl : pkg.genericInstantiatedDecls) {
   139→        // we only collect local const func decl
   140→        if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL && decl->IsConst() &&
   141→            IsLocalFunc(*StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(decl.get()))) {
   142→            instLocalconstFuncs.emplace_back(StaticCast<AST::FuncDecl*>(decl.get()));
   143→        }
   144→    }
   145→    collector.Collect(instLocalconstFuncs, false);
   146→
   147→    for (const auto decl : collector.GetLocalConstFuncDecls()) {
   148→        localConstFuncs.AddElement(decl);
   149→    }
   150→    for (const auto decl : collector.GetLocalConstVarDecls()) {
   151→        localConstVars.AddElement(decl);
   152→    }
   153→}
   154→
   155→std::pair<InitOrder, bool> AST2CHIR::SortGlobalVarDecl(const AST::Package& pkg)
   156→{
   157→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "SortGlobalVarDecl");
   158→
   159→    CollectStaticInitFuncInfo();
   160→    CollectFuncsAndVars();
   161→    CollectLocalConstFuncAndVars(pkg);
   162→
   163→    ElementList<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> nodesWithDeps;
   164→    for (auto element : funcsAndVars.stableOrderValue) {
   165→        // We will skip those non-recompiled decls in incremental compilation cause they will have no body to be
   166→        // analyze, but the desugar generated `$init` should be kept specially cause it has body
   167→        if (kind == IncreKind::INCR && !element->toBeCompiled && element->identifier != STATIC_INIT_VAR) {
   168→            continue;
   169→        }
   170→        nodesWithDeps.AddElement(element);
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    auto analysis = GlobalDeclAnalysis(
   174→        diag, gim, kind, funcsAndVars, localConstVars, staticInitFuncInfoMap, outputCHIR, mergingSpecific);
   175→    auto initOrder = analysis.Run(nodesWithDeps, fileAndVarMap, cachedInfo);
   176→
   177→    // Speically, now we want to flattern the local const VarWithPattern decl which will be useful in translation later.
   178→    // Also we need to set these local const vars with `Recompile` flag for the sake of incremental compilation.
   179→    ElementList<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> flatternedLocalConstVars;
   180→    for (auto& element : localConstVars.stableOrderValue) {
   181→        if (element->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL) {
   182→            (const_cast<AST::Decl*>(element.get()))->toBeCompiled = true;
   183→            flatternedLocalConstVars.AddElement(element);
   184→        } else if (auto varWithPattern = DynamicCast<const AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(element)) {
   185→            (const_cast<AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(varWithPattern))->toBeCompiled = true;
   186→            auto allPatterns = FlattenVarWithPatternDecl(*varWithPattern);
   187→            for (auto pattern : allPatterns) {
   188→                if (pattern->astKind != AST::ASTKind::VAR_PATTERN) {
   189→                    continue;
   190→                }
   191→                auto varPattern = StaticCast<AST::VarPattern*>(pattern);
   192→                varPattern->varDecl->toBeCompiled = true;
   193→                flatternedLocalConstVars.AddElement(varPattern->varDecl);
   194→            }
   195→        }
   196→    }
   197→    localConstVars = std::move(flatternedLocalConstVars);
   198→
   199→    // If we find circular dependency, return false
   200→    bool result = diag.GetErrorCount() == 0;
   201→    return std::make_pair(initOrder, result);
   202→}
   203→
   204→void AST2CHIR::CreateGlobalVarSignature(const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls, bool isLocalConst)
   205→{
   206→    for (auto& decl : decls) {
   207→        CJC_ASSERT(decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL || decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_WITH_PATTERN_DECL);
   208→        if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL) {
   209→            CreateAndCacheGlobalVar(*StaticCast<const AST::VarDecl*>(decl), isLocalConst);
   210→        } else if (decl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_WITH_PATTERN_DECL) {
   211→            FlatternPattern(*(StaticCast<const AST::VarWithPatternDecl*>(decl)->irrefutablePattern), isLocalConst);
   212→        }
   213→    }
   214→}
   215→
   216→void AST2CHIR::FlatternPattern(const AST::Pattern& pattern, bool isLocalConst)
   217→{
   218→    switch (pattern.astKind) {
   219→        case AST::ASTKind::VAR_PATTERN: {
   220→            auto varPattern = StaticCast<const AST::VarPattern*>(&pattern);
   221→            auto varDecl = varPattern->varDecl.get();
   222→            CreateAndCacheGlobalVar(*varDecl, isLocalConst);
   223→            break;
   224→        }
   225→        case AST::ASTKind::TUPLE_PATTERN: {
   226→            auto tuplePattern = StaticCast<const AST::TuplePattern*>(&pattern);
   227→            for (auto& subPattern : tuplePattern->patterns) {
   228→                FlatternPattern(*subPattern, isLocalConst);
   229→            }
   230→            break;
   231→        }
   232→        case AST::ASTKind::ENUM_PATTERN: {
   233→            auto enumPattern = StaticCast<const AST::EnumPattern*>(&pattern);
   234→            for (auto& subPattern : enumPattern->patterns) {
   235→                FlatternPattern(*subPattern, isLocalConst);
   236→            }
   237→            break;
   238→        }
   239→        case AST::ASTKind::WILDCARD_PATTERN: {
   240→            break;
   241→        }
   242→        default: {
   243→            Errorln("decl with unsupported pattern");
   244→            CJC_ABORT();
   245→        }
   246→    }
   247→}
   248→
   249→void AST2CHIR::SetInitFuncForStaticVar()
   250→{
   251→    for (auto& skipedStaticVar : varsInitedByStaticInitFunc) {
   252→        // If common var with specific one, need to skip
   253→        auto skipedStaticVarVal = globalCache.TryGet(*skipedStaticVar);
   254→        if (skipedStaticVarVal == nullptr || skipedStaticVar->specificImplementation) {
   255→            continue;
   256→        }
   257→        CJC_ASSERT(skipedStaticVar->astKind == AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL);
   258→        // Also set the init func here
   259→        if (auto skipedStaticVarInCHIR = DynamicCast<GlobalVar*>(skipedStaticVarVal)) {
   260→            auto staticInitFuncInAST = staticInitFuncInfoMap.at(skipedStaticVar->outerDecl).staticInitFunc;
   261→            auto staticInitFuncInCHIR = DynamicCast<Func*>(globalCache.Get(*staticInitFuncInAST));
   262→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(staticInitFuncInCHIR);
   263→            skipedStaticVarInCHIR->SetInitFunc(*staticInitFuncInCHIR);
   264→        }
   265→    }
   266→}
   267→
   268→Translator AST2CHIR::CreateTranslator()
   269→{
   270→    return Translator{builder, chirType, opts, gim, globalCache, localConstVars, localConstFuncs, kind,
   271→        deserializedVals, annoFactoryFuncs, maybeUnreachable, isComputingAnnos, initFuncsForAnnoFactory, types};
   272→}
   273→
   274→void AST2CHIR::TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   275→{
   276→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateInitOfGlobalVars");
   277→    auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   278→    GlobalVarInitializer initializer(trans, importManager, initFuncsForConstVar, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   279→    initializer.Run(pkg, initOrder);
   280→    SetInitFuncForStaticVar();
   281→}
   282→
   283→void AST2CHIR::CollectTopLevelDecls(AST::Package& pkg)
   284→{
   285→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "CollectTopLevelDecls");
   286→    // For some special functions, they are explicitly imported even they are NOT explicitly used.
   287→    // Collect implicit imported/used decl, the decl list is made by
   288→    // `REG_IMPLICIT_IMPORTED_NON_GENERIC_FUNC` and `REG_IMPLICIT_IMPORTED_GENERIC_FUNC`,there are two cases:
   289→    //   1. if `pkg` is not std.core, we collect implicit imported decls, especially those generic decl in std.core, but
   290→    //   instantiated decls in other imported package.
   291→    //   2. if `pkg` is std.core (aka we are compiling std.core), we collect implicit used decls by down stream package.
   292→    CollectImplicitFuncs();
   293→
   294→    // Collect Imported Pkg Top-Level Decl Part
   295→    CollectImportedDecls(pkg);
   296→
   297→    // Collect Current Pkg Top-Level Decl & Generic Top-Level Decl Part
   298→    CollectDeclsInCurPkg(pkg);
   299→}
   300→
   301→void AST2CHIR::CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable()
   302→{
   303→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable");
   304→    // translate all custom type decl, and cache them to global symbol table
   305→    // only create a shell of `CustomTypeDef`, including its ptr and attribute, not fill its method, vtable and so on
   306→    CacheCustomTypeDefToGlobalSymbolTable();
   307→    // translate all custom type's type, and set type to `CustomTypeDef`
   308→    TranslateAllCustomTypeTy();
   309→    // create all top-level func decl's shell and var decls, cache them to global symbol table.
   310→    CacheTopLevelDeclToGlobalSymbolTable();
   311→
   312→    SetGenericDecls();
   313→}
   314→
   315→void AST2CHIR::SetGenericDecls() const
   316→{
   317→    if (!gim) {
   318→        return;
   319→    }
   320→    auto genericToInsMap = gim->GetAllGenericToInsDecls();
   321→    for (auto& mapIt : genericToInsMap) {
   322→        if (mapIt.first->astKind == AST::ASTKind::EXTEND_DECL) {
   323→            continue;
   324→        }
   325→        if (mapIt.first->IsNominalDecl()) {
   326→            auto chirGeneric = chirType.TryGetGlobalNominalCache(*mapIt.first);
   327→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(chirGeneric);
   328→            for (auto insDecl : mapIt.second) {
   329→                auto chirIns = chirType.TryGetGlobalNominalCache(*insDecl);
   330→                // instantiated decl may be imported but not used in current package, so it's not translated by CHIR
   331→                if (chirIns == nullptr) {
   332→                    continue;
   333→                }
   334→                chirIns->SetGenericDecl(*chirGeneric);
   335→            }
   336→        } else if (mapIt.first->astKind == AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   337→            auto chirGeneric = globalCache.TryGet(*mapIt.first);
   338→            // intrinsic
   339→            if (chirGeneric == nullptr) {
   340→                continue;
   341→            }
   342→            for (auto insDecl : mapIt.second) {
   343→                auto chirIns = globalCache.TryGet(*insDecl);
   344→                // shouldn't be nullptr
   345→                if (chirIns == nullptr) {
   346→                    continue;
   347→                }
   348→                VirtualCast<FuncBase*>(chirIns)->SetGenericDecl(*VirtualCast<FuncBase*>(chirGeneric));
   349→            }
   350→        }
   351→    }
   352→}
   353→
   354→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl)
   355→{
   356→    if (decl.astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   357→        return;
   358→    }
   359→    // const_cast is safe: we own the AST tree and are past the translation point for this decl.
   360→    auto& funcDecl = const_cast<AST::FuncDecl&>(static_cast<const AST::FuncDecl&>(decl));
   361→    if (funcDecl.funcBody != nullptr && funcDecl.funcBody->body != nullptr) {
   362→        funcDecl.funcBody->body.reset();
   363→    }
   364→}
   365→
   366→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl)
   367→{
   368→    if (decl.initializer != nullptr) {
   369→        decl.initializer.reset();
   370→    }
   371→}
   372→
   373→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& /* pkg */)
   374→{
   375→    // Release method bodies from nominal decls (class/interface/struct/enum) after batch translation.
   376→    // Uses GetMemberDecls() which is the canonical way to access members across all nominal types.
   377→    auto releaseMethodBodies = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls) {
   378→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   379→            auto& memberDecls = decl->GetMemberDecls();
   380→            for (auto& member : memberDecls) {
   381→                ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   382→            }
   383→        }
   384→    };
   385→    releaseMethodBodies(nominalDecls);
   386→    releaseMethodBodies(genericNominalDecls);
   387→}
   388→
   389→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder)
   390→{
   391→    for (auto& [file, decls] : initOrder) {
   392→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   393→            if (auto* varDecl = DynamicCast<AST::VarDeclAbstract*>(const_cast<AST::Decl*>(decl.get()))) {
   394→                ReleaseVarInitializer(*varDecl);
   395→            }
   396→        }
   397→    }
   398→}
   399→
   400→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies()
   401→{
   402→    for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   403→        if (NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   404→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   405→        }
   406→    }
   407→    for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   408→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   409→    }
   410→}
   411→
   412→void AST2CHIR::TranslateAllDecls(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   413→{
   414→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "TranslateAllDecls");
   415→    // step 1: translate nominal decls first (signatures only — method bodies are translated in step 3)
   416→    TranslateNominalDecls(pkg);
   417→    // NOTE: Do NOT call ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies() here.
   418→    // TranslateNominalDecls only translates signatures (types, params, attributes).
   419→    // Method bodies are translated in step 3 via globalAndMemberFuncs, and released there
   420→    // by ReleaseFuncBody (serial) or ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies (parallel).
   421→    // Releasing here would null funcBody->body before step 3 translates it,
   422→    // causing null pointer dereference in HasDelegatedThisCall / TranslateNestedFunc.
   423→
   424→    // step 2: translate initialization of global var
   425→    TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(pkg, initOrder);
   426→    ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(initOrder);
   427→
   428→    // do this after init of gv to ensure gvinit of CustomAnnotations go after real gv's
   429→    // this is always safe because such gvinit's are generated by CHIR and cannot be referenced in source
   430→    for (auto decl : annoOnlyDecls) {
   431→        CreateAnnoOnlyDeclSig(*decl);
   432→    }
   433→
   434→    // step 3: translate body of all funcs, the process can be run in parallel according to the compilation option
   435→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   436→    if (opts.GetJobs() > 1) {
   437→        TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel();
   438→        ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();
   439→    } else {
   440→        for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   441→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   442→                continue;
   443→            }
   444→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   445→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   446→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   447→            if (decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GLOBAL)) {
   448→                trans.CollectValueAnnotation(*decl);
   449→            }
   450→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   451→        }
   452→        for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   453→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   454→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   455→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   456→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   457→        }
   458→    }
   459→    // the parallel helper does not accept this type, use serialised translation
   460→    for (auto decl : annoFactoryFuncs) {
   461→        auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   462→        trans.SetTopLevel(*decl.first);
   463→        trans.TranslateAnnoFactoryFuncBody(*decl.first, *decl.second);
   464→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl.first);
   465→    }
   466→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   467→
   468→    // step 4: set `CompileTimeValue` for lambda — operates on CHIR IR, unaffected by AST release
   469→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   470→    for (auto func : package->GetGlobalFuncs()) {
   471→        if (func->TestAttr(Attribute::CONST)) {
   472→            SetCompileTimeValueFlagRecursivly(*func);
   473→        }
   474→    }
   475→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   476→}
   477→
   478→void AST2CHIR::TranslateInParallel(const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls)
   479→{
   480→    Utils::ParallelUtil allDeclsParallel(builder, opts.GetJobs());
   481→    allDeclsParallel.RunAST2CHIRInParallel(decls, chirType, opts, gim, globalCache, localConstVars, localConstFuncs,
   482→        kind, deserializedVals, Translator::TranslateASTNode, maybeUnreachable, isComputingAnnos,
   483→        initFuncsForAnnoFactory, types, annoFactoryFuncs);
   484→}
   485→
   486→void AST2CHIR::TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel()
   487→{
   488→    // collect all top-level funcs into a vector.
   489→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> allDecls;
   490→    auto needTrans = [this](Ptr<const AST::Decl> decl) { return NeedTranslate(*decl); };
   491→    // Filter out decls that do not require translation.
   492→    std::copy_if(globalAndMemberFuncs.begin(), globalAndMemberFuncs.end(),
   493→        std::back_inserter(allDecls), needTrans);
   494→    TranslateInParallel(allDecls);
   495→
   496→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> localFuncsGeneric; // generic decls
   497→    std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> localFuncsOther; // instantiated or non-generic decls
   498→    for (auto func : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   499→        if (func->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC)) {
   500→            localFuncsGeneric.push_back(func);
   501→        } else {
   502→            localFuncsOther.push_back(func);
   503→        }
   504→    }
   505→    TranslateInParallel(localFuncsGeneric);
   506→    TranslateInParallel(localFuncsOther);
   507→}
   508→
   509→void AST2CHIR::AST2CHIRCheck()
   510→{
   511→    if (!opts.chirWFC) {
   512→        return;
   513→    }
   514→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "AST2CHIRCheck");
   515→    // check customDefTypes
   516→    auto customDefMap = chirType.GetAllTypeDef();
   517→    for (auto& it : customDefMap) {
   518→        const AST::Node& astNode = *it.first;
   519→        const CHIR::CustomTypeDef& chirNode = *it.second;
   520→        if (astNode.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC, AST::Attribute::IMPORTED)) {
   521→            continue;
   522→        }
   523→        if (astNode.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::IMPORTED) && chirNode.TestAttr(Attribute::DESERIALIZED)) {
   524→            continue;
   525→        }
   526→        if (chirNode.TestAttr(Attribute::SKIP_ANALYSIS)) {
   527→            continue;
   528→        }
   529→        auto ret = AST2CHIRCheckCustomTypeDef(astNode, chirNode, globalCache);
   530→        if (!ret) {
   531→            this->failure = true;
   532→            it.second->Dump();
   533→        }
   534→    }
   535→    // check globalFunc and globalVar
   536→    for (auto& it : globalCache.GetALL()) {
   537→        if (it.second->TestAttr(Attribute::SKIP_ANALYSIS)) {
   538→            continue;
   539→        }
   540→        auto ret = AST2CHIRCheckValue(*it.first, *it.second);
   541→        if (!ret) {
   542→            this->failure = true;
   543→            it.second->Dump();
   544→        }
   545→    }
   546→}
   547→
   548→/// Return true if chir was deserialized
   549→bool AST2CHIR::TryToDeserializeCHIR()
   550→{
   551→    auto& chirFiles = opts.inputChirFiles;
   552→    CJC_ASSERT(chirFiles.size() != 0);
   553→    ToCHIR::Phase phase;
   554→    bool success = true;
   555→    for (auto chirFile : chirFiles) {
   556→        success &= CHIRDeserializer::Deserialize(chirFile, builder, phase, true);
   557→        mergingSpecific = true;
   558→    }
   559→    return success;
   560→}
   561→
   562→static Package::AccessLevel BuildPackageAccessLevel(const AST::AccessLevel& level)
   563→{
   564→    static std::unordered_map<AST::AccessLevel, Package::AccessLevel> accessLevelMap = {
   565→        {AST::AccessLevel::INTERNAL, Package::AccessLevel::INTERNAL},
   566→        {AST::AccessLevel::PROTECTED, Package::AccessLevel::PROTECTED},
   567→        {AST::AccessLevel::PUBLIC, Package::AccessLevel::PUBLIC},
   568→    };
   569→
   570→    auto it = accessLevelMap.find(level);
   571→    CJC_ASSERT(it != accessLevelMap.end());
   572→    return it->second;
   573→}
   574→
   575→bool AST2CHIR::ToCHIRPackage(AST::Package& node)
   576→{
   577→    // It can be not null in case of part of the package was deserialized from .chir
   578→    bool needDesCHIR = opts.inputChirFiles.size() != 0;
   579→    if (!needDesCHIR) {
   580→        package = builder.CreatePackage(node.fullPackageName);
   581→        outputCHIR = opts.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR;
   582→    } else if (TryToDeserializeCHIR()) {
   583→        package = builder.GetCurPackage();
   584→        BuildDeserializedTable();
   585→    } else {
   586→        return false;
   587→    }
   588→    // Translating common alongside with merging specific is not supported
   589→    CJC_ASSERT(!(outputCHIR && mergingSpecific));
   590→    package->SetPackageAccessLevel(BuildPackageAccessLevel(node.accessible));
   591→    RegisterAllSources();
   592→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(package);
   593→    dependencyPkg = importManager.GetAllDependentPackageNames(node.fullPackageName);
   594→
   595→    // step 1: collect all top-level decls
   596→    CollectTopLevelDecls(node);
   597→
   598→    // step 2: sort and do circular dependency checking
   599→    auto [initOrder, result] = SortGlobalVarDecl(node);
   600→    if (!result) {
   601→        return false;
   602→    }
   603→
   604→    // step 3: create signature of nominal decls and top-level func decls
   605→    CacheSomeDeclsToGlobalSymbolTable();
   606→
   607→    // step 4: translate all colleted decls
   608→    TranslateAllDecls(node, initOrder);
   609→
   610→    // step 5: ast2chir check
   611→    AST2CHIRCheck();
   612→
   613→    return !HasFailed();
   614→}
   615→} // namespace Cangjie::CHIR
   616→
```

</details>

```
   442→    // SrcCodeChangeState
   443→    enum class SrcCodeChangeState : uint8_t {
   444→        UNCHANGED = 0,
   445→        CHANGED = 1,
   446→        ADDED = 2,
   447→        DELETED = 3,
   448→    };
   449→    struct SrcCodeCacheInfo {
   450→        SrcCodeChangeState state{SrcCodeChangeState::ADDED};
   451→        std::string code;
   452→        SrcCodeCacheInfo() = default;
   453→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeCacheInfo&& info) = default;
   454→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(const SrcCodeCacheInfo& info) = default;
   455→        SrcCodeCacheInfo& operator=(SrcCodeCacheInfo&& info) = default;
   456→        SrcCodeCacheInfo& operator=(const SrcCodeCacheInfo& info) = default;
   457→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(const std::string& code) : code(code) {};
   458→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(std::string&& code) : code(std::move(code)) {};
   459→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeChangeState state, const std::string& code) : state(state), code(code) {};
   460→        SrcCodeCacheInfo(SrcCodeChangeState state, std::string&& code) : state(state), code(std::move(code)) {};
   461→    };

   474→     * @brief Get the CHIRContext
   475→     */
   476→    CHIR::CHIRContext& GetCHIRContext();
   477→
   478→    /**
   479→     * @brief Get astPkg2chirPkgMap
   480→     */
   481→    const std::unordered_map<Ptr<AST::Package>, Ptr<CHIR::Package>>& GetASTPkg2CHIRPkgMap()
   482→    {
   483→        return astPkg2chirPkgMap;
   484→    }
   485→
   486→#ifdef CANGJIE_CODEGEN_CJNATIVE_BACKEND
   487→    // used only by cjlint
   488→    const CHIR::ConstAnalysisWrapper& GetConstAnalysisWrapper() const;
   489→
   490→    std::vector<CHIR::Package*> GetAllCHIRPackages() const;
   491→#else

   494→    {
   495→        return constAnalysisWrapper;
   496→    }
   497→    std::vector<CHIR::Package*> GetAllCHIRPackages() const
   498→    {

   500→        for (auto& it : astPkg2chirPkgMap) {
   501→            res.emplace_back(it.second);
   502→        }
   503→        return res;
   504→    }
   505→#endif
   506→
   507→    /**
   508→     * @brief mangler
   509→     */
   510→    std::unique_ptr<BaseMangler> mangler;
   511→
   512→    /**
   513→     * Map between the mangle name (before sema) with the Decl.
   514→     */
   515→    std::map<std::string, Ptr<AST::Decl>> mangledName2DeclMap;
   516→
   517→    // Every compiler instance has a source manager.
   518→    SourceManager sm;
   519→
   520→    /// Incremental compilation state.
   521→    IncreKind kind{IncreKind::INVALID};
   522→
   523→    ///@{
   524→    /// Overriden by CJLint
   525→    bool releaseCHIRMemory = true;
   526→    bool needToOptString = false;
   527→    bool needToOptGenericDecl = false;
   528→    bool isCJLint = false;
   529→    ///@}
   530→
   531→    /************** Used by Incremental Compilation Start **************/
   532→    RawMangled2DeclMap rawMangleName2DeclMap;
   533→    ASTCache astCacheInfo;
   534→    std::unordered_set<Ptr<const AST::Decl>> declsWithDuplicatedRawMangleName;
   535→    std::unordered_map<RawMangledName, std::list<std::pair<Ptr<AST::ExtendDecl>, int>>> directExtends;
   536→    FileMap fileMap;
   537→    std::vector<const AST::Decl*> order;

   541→    {

   543→    }

   548→    }
   549→
   550→    /**

   552→     * Decouples CodeGen from srcPkgs so it works after AST is freed.
   553→     */
   554→    struct PackageCodeGenInfo {

   556→        bool isEmpty = false;
   557→    };

   559→    /// Public accessors for AST release state, used by DefaultCIImpl and subclasses.

   573→    std::unordered_map<Ptr<AST::Package>, Ptr<CHIR::Package>> astPkg2chirPkgMap;
   574→#endif
   575→    bool HasTypeChecker() const
   576→    {
   577→        return typeChecker != nullptr;
   578→    }
   579→

   605→     *
   606→     * Clears AST nodes, ASTContext, managers, and all dangling AST pointer holders.
   607→     * Destruction order: CHIR refs → CompilerInstance members → managers → AST core.
   608→     */
   609→    void ReleaseASTMemory();
```

```
     1→// Copyright (c) Huawei Technologies Co., Ltd. 2025. All rights reserved.
     2→// This source file is part of the Cangjie project, licensed under Apache-2.0
     3→// with Runtime Library Exception.
     4→//
     5→// See https://cangjie-lang.cn/pages/LICENSE for license information.
     6→
     7→#include "cangjie/AST/Node.h"
     8→#include "cangjie/AST/Utils.h"
     9→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/TranslateASTNode/Translator.h"
    10→#include "cangjie/CHIR/AST2CHIR/Utils.h"
    11→#include "cangjie/CHIR/IR/AttributeInfo.h"
    12→#include "cangjie/CHIR/Utils/Utils.h"
    13→
    14→#include <mutex>
    15→static std::mutex g_memberVarMutex;
    16→namespace Cangjie::CHIR {
    17→using namespace AST;
    18→
    19→void Translator::BindingFuncParam(
    20→    const AST::FuncParamList& paramList, const BlockGroup& funcBody, const BindingConfig& cfg)
    21→{
    22→    const auto& params = GetFuncParams(funcBody);
    23→    size_t offset = paramList.params.size() < params.size() ? 1 : 0;
    24→    CJC_ASSERT(paramList.params.size() + offset == params.size());
    25→    auto block = funcBody.GetEntryBlock();
    26→    for (size_t i = 0; i < paramList.params.size(); ++i) {
    27→        auto arg = params[i + offset];
    28→        auto& param = paramList.params[i];
    29→        if (cfg.setSymbol) {
    30→            SetSymbolTable(*param, *arg);
    31→        }
    32→        if (!cfg.createDebug) {
    33→            continue;
    34→        }
    35→        auto loc = TranslateLocation(*param);
    36→        auto paramLoc = GetDeclLoc(builder.GetChirContext(), *param);
    37→        // Don't need to report unused parameter on defaut value parameter function.
    38→        auto debug = CreateAndAppendExpression<Debug>(
    39→            paramLoc, loc, builder.GetUnitTy(), arg, param->identifier.GetRawText(), block);
    40→        if (cfg.hasInitial) {
    41→            debug->Set<SkipCheck>(SkipKind::SKIP_DCE_WARNING);
    42→        }
    43→    }
    44→}
    45→
    46→static Ptr<AST::Decl> GetGenericDecl(const AST::Decl* instantiation)
    47→{
    48→    if (instantiation == nullptr) {
    49→        return nullptr;
    50→    }
    51→    if (instantiation->outerDecl && instantiation->outerDecl->genericDecl) {
    52→        return instantiation->outerDecl->genericDecl;
    53→    }
    54→    if (instantiation->genericDecl) {
    55→        return instantiation->genericDecl;
    56→    }
    57→    return nullptr;
    58→}
    59→
    60→static bool IsCopiedSrcFuncFromInterface(const AST::Decl* decl)
    61→{
    62→    if (decl == nullptr) {
    63→        return false;
    64→    }
    65→    // Imported copied function will have rawMangled name, and do not need to record its parent.
    66→    return decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::DEFAULT, AST::Attribute::COMPILER_ADD) && decl->outerDecl != nullptr &&
    67→        !decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::IMPORTED);
    68→}
    69→
    70→static bool IsMemberFuncOfBox(const AST::Decl* decl)
    71→{
    72→    if (decl == nullptr) {
    73→        return false;
    74→    }
    75→    if (decl->astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL || decl->outerDecl == nullptr) {
    76→        return false;
    77→    }
    78→    return decl->outerDecl->identifier.Val().find("$BOX_") != std::string::npos;
    79→}
    80→
    81→static bool IsMemberFuncOfExtend(const AST::Decl* decl)
    82→{
    83→    if (decl == nullptr) {
    84→        return false;
    85→    }
    86→    if (decl->astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL || decl->outerDecl == nullptr) {
    87→        return false;
    88→    }
    89→    return decl->outerDecl->astKind == AST::ASTKind::EXTEND_DECL;
    90→}
    91→
    92→void Translator::SetRawMangledNameForIncrementalCompile(const AST::FuncDecl& astFunc, Func& chirFunc) const
    93→{
    94→    AST::Decl* decl = nullptr;
    95→    if (astFunc.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::HAS_INITIAL)) {
    96→        // this func is default param of another func, so it doesn't have rawMangledName
    97→        // if this func need to be recompiled, we need to recompile its owner func
    98→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(astFunc.ownerFunc);
    99→        decl = astFunc.ownerFunc;
   100→    }
   101→
   102→    // this func is a member method of class, and copied from interface, so it doesn't have rawMangledName
   103→    // if this func need to be recompiled, we need to recompile its class
   104→    if (IsCopiedSrcFuncFromInterface(decl)) {
   105→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(decl);
   106→        decl = decl->outerDecl;
   107→    } else if (IsCopiedSrcFuncFromInterface(&astFunc)) {
   108→        decl = astFunc.outerDecl;
   109→    }
   110→
   111→    // this func is a member method of BOX, so it doesn't have rawMangledName
   112→    // if this func need to be recompiled, we need to recompile its class
   113→    if (IsMemberFuncOfBox(decl)) {
   114→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(decl);
   115→        decl = decl->outerDecl;
   116→    } else if (IsMemberFuncOfBox(&astFunc)) {
   117→        decl = astFunc.outerDecl;
   118→    }
   119→
   120→    AST::Decl* parent = nullptr;
   121→    if (IsMemberFuncOfExtend(decl)) {
   122→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(decl);
   123→        parent = decl->outerDecl;
   124→    } else if (IsMemberFuncOfExtend(&astFunc)) {
   125→        parent = astFunc.outerDecl;
   126→    }
   127→
   128→    // this func is a instantiated func, so it doesn't have rawMangledName
   129→    // if this func need to be recompiled, we need to recompile its generic decl
   130→    if (auto gd1 = GetGenericDecl(decl); gd1) {
   131→        decl = gd1;
   132→    } else if (auto gd2 = GetGenericDecl(&astFunc); gd2) {
   133→        decl = gd2;
   134→    } else if (auto gd3 = GetGenericDecl(parent); gd3) {
   135→        parent = gd3;
   136→    }
   137→
   138→    if (decl != nullptr) {
   139→        if (decl->identifier.Val().find("$BOX_") != std::string::npos) {
   140→            chirFunc.SetRawMangledName("$BOX");
   141→        } else {
   142→            chirFunc.SetRawMangledName(decl->rawMangleName);
   143→        }
   144→    } else {
   145→        chirFunc.SetRawMangledName(astFunc.rawMangleName);
   146→    }
   147→}
   148→
   149→bool NeedCreateDebugForFirstParam(const Func& func)
   150→{
   151→    if (func.TestAttr(Attribute::STATIC)) {
   152→        return false;
   153→    }
   154→    auto parentDef = func.GetParentCustomTypeDef();
   155→    // global function doesn't have `this`
   156→    if (parentDef == nullptr) {
   157→        return false;
   158→    }
   159→    auto extendDef = DynamicCast<ExtendDef*>(parentDef);
   160→    // function declared in class, struct, enum def need create `Debug(%0, this)`
   161→    if (extendDef == nullptr) {
   162→        return true;
   163→    }
   164→    // function declared in `extend Int32` doesn't need to create `Debug(%0, this)`, it's better in cjdb
   165→    return extendDef->GetExtendedType()->IsNominal();
   166→}
   167→
   168→Ptr<Value> Translator::Visit(const AST::FuncDecl& func)
   169→{
   170→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(func.funcBody);
   171→    // Abstract function do not need func body. 'intrinsic' and 'foreign' function was ignored from toplevel.
   172→    if (func.TestAnyAttr(AST::Attribute::INTRINSIC, AST::Attribute::ABSTRACT, AST::Attribute::FOREIGN)) {
   173→        return nullptr;
   174→    }
   175→    if (IsCommonWithoutDefault(func)) {
   176→        return nullptr;
   177→    }
   178→    bool isLifted = localConstFuncs.HasElement(&func);
   179→    if (isLifted && !IsTopLevel(func)) {
   180→        return nullptr;
   181→    }
   182→    if ((func.ownerFunc ? !IsGlobalOrMember(*func.ownerFunc) : !IsGlobalOrMember(func)) && !isLifted) {
   183→        // local const funcs are lifted to global funcs, do not translate as nested func
   184→        return TranslateNestedFunc(func);
   185→    }
   186→    // In incremental compilation, no need to generate body for non-recompile func, but we need to
   187→    // exclude the nested func here
   188→    if (increKind == IncreKind::INCR && !func.toBeCompiled && !IsSrcCodeImportedGlobalDecl(func, opts)) {
   189→        return nullptr;
   190→    }
   191→    CJC_ASSERT(!isLifted || IsTopLevel(func));
   192→    // translateTopLevel
   193→    Func* curFunc = VirtualCast<Func*>(globalSymbolTable.Get(func));
   194→    if (IsCopiedSrcFuncFromInterface(&func)) {
   195→        curFunc->Set<SkipCheck>(SkipKind::SKIP_DCE_WARNING);
   196→    }
   197→    SetRawMangledNameForIncrementalCompile(func, *curFunc);
   198→    if (curFunc->GetFuncKind() == FuncKind::GETTER || curFunc->GetFuncKind() == FuncKind::SETTER) {
   199→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(func.propDecl);
   200→        auto propLoc = TranslateLocation(*func.propDecl);
   201→        curFunc->SetPropLocation(propLoc);
   202→    }
   203→
   204→    auto body = curFunc->GetBody();
   205→    blockGroupStack.emplace_back(body);
   206→    auto entry = builder.CreateBlock(body);
   207→    body->SetEntryBlock(entry);
   208→    if (NeedCreateDebugForFirstParam(*curFunc)) {
   209→        auto thisVar = curFunc->GetParam(0);
   210→        CreateAndAppendExpression<Debug>(builder.GetUnitTy(), thisVar, "this", curFunc->GetEntryBlock());
   211→    }
   212→    BindingFuncParam(*func.funcBody->paramLists[0], *curFunc->GetBody(),
   213→        {.hasInitial = func.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::HAS_INITIAL), .createDebug = true});
   214→    // Set return value if the return type is not Void
   215→    auto retType = curFunc->GetReturnType();
   216→    if (!retType->IsVoid()) {
   217→        auto retVal =
   218→            CreateAndAppendExpression<Allocate>(DebugLocation(), builder.GetType<RefType>(retType), retType, entry)
   219→                ->GetResult();
   220→        curFunc->SetReturnValue(*retVal);
   221→    }
   222→    // Translate body.
   223→    auto block = Visit(*func.funcBody.get());
   224→    CreateAndAppendTerminator<GoTo>(StaticCast<Block*>(block.get()), entry);
   225→    blockGroupStack.pop_back();
   226→    return curFunc;
   227→}
   228→
   229→Ptr<Value> Translator::Visit(const AST::FuncBody& funcBody)
   230→{
   231→    Ptr<Value> ret{nullptr};
   232→    if (funcBody.funcDecl == nullptr) {
   233→        // Translate lambda body (lambda body is treated as normal func body).
   234→        ret = TranslateFuncBody(funcBody);
   235→    } else {
   236→        auto func = funcBody.funcDecl;
   237→        if (IsInstanceConstructor(*func)) {
   238→            CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(func->outerDecl);
   239→            if (func->outerDecl->TestAnyAttr(AST::Attribute::COMMON, AST::Attribute::SPECIFIC)) {
   240→                ret = TranslateConstructorFunc(*func->outerDecl, funcBody);
   241→            } else {
   242→                ret = TranslateConstructorFuncInline(*func->outerDecl, funcBody);
   243→            }
   244→        } else if (IsInstanceMember(*func)) {
   245→            ret = TranslateInstanceMemberFunc(*func->outerDecl, funcBody);
   246→        } else {
   247→            // Translate normal function
   248→            ret = TranslateFuncBody(funcBody);
   249→        }
   250→    }
   251→
   252→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(ret);
   253→    return ret;
   254→}
   255→
   256→Ptr<Block> Translator::TranslateFuncBody(const AST::FuncBody& funcBody)
   257→{
   258→    if (funcBody.body == nullptr) {
   259→        return CreateBlock();
   260→    }
   261→    CJC_ASSERT(funcBody.body);
   262→    Visit(*funcBody.body);
   263→    CJC_ASSERT(currentBlock);
   264→    // After translation of body,
   265→    // if the last block is an unreachable block, it may not have terminator and will be removed later,
   266→    // otherwise it must have a terminator.
   267→    CJC_ASSERT((!currentBlock->IsEntry() && currentBlock->GetPredecessors().empty()) ||
   268→        currentBlock->GetTerminator() != nullptr);
   269→    return GetBlockByAST(*funcBody.body);
   270→}
   271→
   272→Ptr<Value> Translator::TranslateInstanceMemberFunc(const AST::Decl& parent, const AST::FuncBody& funcBody)
   273→{
   274→    auto curFunc = GetCurrentFunc();
   275→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(curFunc);
   276→    // Binding the implicit 'this' with the first param of the function.
   277→    auto thisVar = curFunc->GetParam(0);
   278→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(thisVar);
   279→    if (parent.astKind == AST::ASTKind::EXTEND_DECL) {
   280→        if (auto typeDecl = AST::Ty::GetDeclOfTy(parent.ty)) {
   281→            SetSymbolTable(*typeDecl, *thisVar);
   282→        }
   283→    } else {
   284→        SetSymbolTable(parent, *thisVar);
   285→    }
   286→    return TranslateFuncBody(funcBody);
   287→}
   288→
   289→namespace {
   290→// Get instance field size of super type. Always return 0 for non-class type.
   291→uint64_t GetSuperInstanceVarSize(const Type& thisType)
   292→{
   293→    CJC_ASSERT(thisType.IsRef());
   294→    auto realType = StaticCast<const RefType&>(thisType).GetBaseType();
   295→    if (!realType->IsClass()) {
   296→        return 0;
   297→    }
   298→    auto super = StaticCast<ClassType*>(realType)->GetClassDef()->GetSuperClassDef();
   299→    return super ? super->GetAllInstanceVarNum() : 0;
   300→}
   301→
   302→// returns true when the function body contains a delegated this constructor call
   303→bool HasDelegatedThisCall(const AST::FuncBody& func)
   304→{
   305→    CJC_ASSERT(func.body);
   306→    auto& body = func.body->body;
   307→    CJC_ASSERT(!body.empty());
   308→    // first expression is callexpr to constructor
   309→    if (auto call = DynamicCast<AST::CallExpr>(body[0].get())) {
   310→        // the `resolvedFunction` of callExpr with call_function_ptr is null.
   311→        if (call->callKind == AST::CallKind::CALL_FUNCTION_PTR) {
   312→            return false;
   313→        }
   314→        /* example code:
   315→         init() {
   316→            this(1)  // we want to find `this` constructor, and recognized by it's baseFunc is 'this' and
   317→        resolvedFunction is constructor.
   318→        }
   319→        */
   320→        if (call->resolvedFunction && call->resolvedFunction->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::CONSTRUCTOR)) {
   321→            // callee is a refexpr that is this
   322→            if (auto ref = DynamicCast<RefExpr>(call->baseFunc.get())) {
   323→                return ref->isThis;
   324→            }
   325→        }
   326→    }
   327→    return false;
   328→}
   329→} // unnamed namespace
   330→
   331→void Translator::TranslateVariablesInit(const AST::Decl& parent, CHIR::Parameter& thisVar)
   332→{
   333→    auto offset = GetSuperInstanceVarSize(*thisVar.GetType());
   334→    CustomTypeDef* typeDef = GetNominalSymbolTable(parent).get();
   335→
   336→    std::unordered_map<std::string, MemberVarInfo*> varInfoByName;
   337→    auto memberVars = typeDef->GetDirectInstanceVars();
   338→    for (auto& varDef : memberVars) {
   339→        varInfoByName.emplace(varDef.name, &varDef);
   340→    }
   341→    auto initOrder = AST::GetVarsInitializationOrderWithPositions(parent);
   342→    for (auto [member, fieldPosition] : initOrder) {
   343→        // Fields declared in primary constructor cannot have initializer
   344→        CJC_ASSERT(!member->isMemberParam || !member->initializer);
   345→
   346→        MemberVarInfo* varInfo = varInfoByName.at(member->identifier);
   347→        if (ShouldTranslateMember(parent, *member)) {
   348→            Translator trans = Copy();
   349→            auto initializerFunc = trans.TranslateVarInit(*member);
   350→            varInfo->initializerFunc = initializerFunc;
   351→        }
   352→
   353→        auto varInitFunc = varInfo->initializerFunc;
   354→        if (varInitFunc) {
   355→            std::vector<Value*> args{&thisVar};
   356→            auto loc = TranslateLocation(*member);
   357→            auto apply = CreateAndAppendExpression<Apply>(
   358→                loc, varInitFunc->GetReturnType(), varInitFunc, FuncCallContext{
   359→                .args = args,
   360→                .thisType = thisVar.GetType()}, currentBlock);
   361→
   362→            auto value = apply->GetResult();
   363→            std::vector<uint64_t> path = {offset + fieldPosition};
   364→            auto pureCurObjType = StaticCast<RefType*>(thisVar.GetType())->GetBaseType();
   365→            CJC_ASSERT(!pureCurObjType->IsRef() && pureCurObjType->IsNominal());
   366→            auto pureCurObjCustomType = StaticCast<CustomType*>(pureCurObjType);
   367→            auto memberType = pureCurObjCustomType->GetInstMemberTypeByPath(path, builder);
   368→            if (value->GetType() == memberType) {
   369→                CreateAndAppendExpression<StoreElementRef>(
   370→                    loc, builder.GetUnitTy(), value, &thisVar, path, currentBlock);
   371→            } else {
   372→                auto castedValue = TypeCastOrBoxIfNeeded(*value, *memberType, loc);
   373→                CreateAndAppendExpression<StoreElementRef>(
   374→                    loc, builder.GetUnitTy(), castedValue, &thisVar, path, currentBlock);
   375→            }
   376→        }
   377→    }
   378→    typeDef->SetDirectInstanceVars(memberVars);
   379→}
   380→
   381→Ptr<Value> Translator::TranslateConstructorFunc(const AST::Decl& parent, const AST::FuncBody& funcBody)
   382→{
   383→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(funcBody.funcDecl);
   384→    auto curFunc = GetCurrentFunc();
   385→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(curFunc);
   386→    // Binding the implicit `this` with the first param of the function.
   387→    auto thisVar = curFunc->GetParam(0);
   388→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(thisVar);
   389→    SetSymbolTable(parent, *thisVar);
   390→    // Create init blocks and initializers for constructor. NOTE: do not create 'GoTo' from entry to init here.
   391→    // Return init block for callee to uniformly create 'GoTo' from entry in 'Visit FuncDecl'.
   392→    auto initBlock = CreateBlock();
   393→    currentBlock = initBlock;
   394→    // insert member decl initializer if this constructor does not have delegate this call
   395→    if (!HasDelegatedThisCall(funcBody)) {
   396→        CustomTypeDef* typeDef = GetNominalSymbolTable(parent).get();
   397→        FuncBase* varInitFunc = typeDef->GetVarInitializationFunc();
   398→        CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(varInitFunc);
   399→        std::vector<Value*> args{thisVar};
   400→        CreateAndAppendExpression<Apply>(DebugLocation(), varInitFunc->GetReturnType(), varInitFunc, FuncCallContext{
   401→            .args = args,
   402→            .thisType = thisVar->GetType()}, currentBlock);
   403→    }
   404→    // After generated the initializers, the 'currentBlock' may change.
   405→    auto lastBlock = currentBlock;
   406→    auto bodyBlock = TranslateFuncBody(funcBody);
   407→    CreateAndAppendTerminator<GoTo>(bodyBlock, lastBlock);
   408→    return initBlock;
   409→}
   410→
   411→Ptr<Value> Translator::TranslateConstructorFuncInline(const AST::Decl& parent, const AST::FuncBody& funcBody)
   412→{
   413→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(funcBody.funcDecl);
   414→    auto curFunc = GetCurrentFunc();
   415→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(curFunc);
   416→    // Binding the implicit `this` with the first param of the function.
   417→    auto thisVar = curFunc->GetParam(0);
   418→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(thisVar);
   419→    SetSymbolTable(parent, *thisVar);
   420→    // Create init blocks and initializers for constructor. NOTE: do not create 'GoTo' from entry to init here.
   421→    // Return init block for callee to uniformly create 'GoTo' from entry in 'Visit FuncDecl'.
   422→    auto initBlock = CreateBlock();
   423→    currentBlock = initBlock;
   424→    // insert member decl initializer if this constructor does not have delegate this call
   425→    if (!HasDelegatedThisCall(funcBody)) {
   426→        auto fieldOffset = GetSuperInstanceVarSize(*thisVar->GetType());
   427→        for (auto member : parent.GetMemberDeclPtrs()) {
   428→            if (member->astKind != AST::ASTKind::VAR_DECL || member->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::STATIC)) {
   429→                continue;
   430→            }
   431→            if (auto& init = StaticCast<AST::VarDecl>(member)->initializer) {
   432→                Ptr<Value> value;
   433→                {
   434→                    std::unique_lock<std::mutex> lock(g_memberVarMutex);
   435→                    value = TranslateExprArg(*init);
   436→                }
   437→                auto loc = TranslateLocation(*member);
   438→                std::vector<uint64_t> path = {fieldOffset};
   439→                auto pureCurObjType = StaticCast<RefType*>(thisVar->GetType())->GetBaseType();
   440→                CJC_ASSERT(!pureCurObjType->IsRef() && pureCurObjType->IsNominal());
   441→                auto pureCurObjCustomType = StaticCast<CustomType*>(pureCurObjType);
   442→                auto memberType = pureCurObjCustomType->GetInstMemberTypeByPath(path, builder);
   443→                if (value->GetType() == memberType) {
   444→                    CreateAndAppendExpression<StoreElementRef>(
   445→                        loc, builder.GetUnitTy(), value, thisVar, path, currentBlock);
   446→                } else {
   447→                    auto castedValue = TypeCastOrBoxIfNeeded(*value, *memberType, loc);
   448→                    CreateAndAppendExpression<StoreElementRef>(
   449→                        loc, builder.GetUnitTy(), castedValue, thisVar, path, currentBlock);
   450→                }
   451→            }
   452→            ++fieldOffset;
   453→        }
   454→    }
   455→    // After generated the initializers, the 'currentBlock' may change.
   456→    auto lastBlock = currentBlock;
   457→    auto bodyBlock = TranslateFuncBody(funcBody);
   458→    CreateAndAppendTerminator<GoTo>(bodyBlock, lastBlock);
   459→    return initBlock;
   460→}
   461→
   462→Ptr<Value> Translator::TranslateNestedFunc(const AST::FuncDecl& func)
   463→{
   464→    CJC_ASSERT(func.funcBody && func.funcBody->body);
   465→    if (func.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC)) {
   466→        TranslateFunctionGenericUpperBounds(chirTy, func);
   467→    }
   468→    auto lambdaTrans = SetupContextForLambda(*func.funcBody->body);
   469→    auto funcTy = RawStaticCast<FuncType*>(TranslateType(*func.ty));
   470→    // Create nested functions' body and parameters.
   471→    CJC_NULLPTR_CHECK(currentBlock->GetTopLevelFunc());
   472→    BlockGroup* body = builder.CreateBlockGroup(*currentBlock->GetTopLevelFunc());
   473→    const auto& loc = TranslateLocation(func);
   474→    std::vector<GenericType*> genericTys;
   475→    // Only collect for generic function which has not been instantiated.
   476→    if (auto generic = func.funcBody->generic.get(); generic && func.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GENERIC)) {
   477→        for (auto& type : generic->typeParameters) {
   478→            genericTys.emplace_back(RawStaticCast<GenericType*>(TranslateType(*type->ty)));
   479→        }
   480→    }
   481→    std::string lambdaMangleName = func.mangledName;
   482→    Lambda* lambda = CreateAndAppendExpression<Lambda>(
   483→        loc, funcTy, funcTy, currentBlock, true, lambdaMangleName, func.identifier, genericTys);
   484→    CJC_ASSERT(lambda);
   485→    lambda->InitBody(*body);
   486→    if (func.isConst) {
   487→        lambda->SetCompileTimeValue();
   488→    }
   489→
   490→    std::vector<DebugLocation> paramLoc;
   491→    for (auto& astParam : func.funcBody->paramLists[0]->params) {
   492→        paramLoc.emplace_back(TranslateLocationWithoutScope(builder.GetChirContext(), astParam->begin, astParam->end));
   493→    }
   494→    auto paramTypes = funcTy->GetParamTypes();
   495→    CJC_ASSERT(paramTypes.size() == paramLoc.size());
   496→    for (size_t i = 0; i < paramTypes.size(); ++i) {
   497→        builder.CreateParameter(paramTypes[i], paramLoc[i], *lambda);
   498→    }
   499→
   500→    SetSymbolTable(func, *lambda->GetResult());
   501→    for (auto& param : func.funcBody->paramLists[0]->params) {
   502→        if (param->desugarDecl) {
   503→            // recursively translate default parameter function of a lambda (possibly a local func)
   504→            auto defaultArgFunc = TranslateNestedFunc(*param->desugarDecl);
   505→            StaticCast<Lambda*>(StaticCast<LocalVar*>(defaultArgFunc)->GetExpr())->SetParamDftValHostFunc(*lambda);
   506→
   507→            // set such functions as local symbols in the current scope but not in the lambda translation context
   508→            // as a default parameter function can only be called outside the function
   509→            lambdaTrans.SetSymbolTable(*param->desugarDecl, *defaultArgFunc);
   510→        }
   511→    }
   512→    // Local function allows to call itself inside funcBody.
   513→    lambdaTrans.SetSymbolTable(func, *lambda->GetResult());
   514→    return lambdaTrans.TranslateLambdaBody(
   515→        lambda, *func.funcBody, {.hasInitial = func.TestAttr(AST::Attribute::HAS_INITIAL)});
   516→}
   517→} // namespace Cangjie::CHIR
   518→
```

```
   405→     */
   406→    bool NeedDumpAST() const;

   513→
   514→    // Built-in package dependencies which analysed by Frontend and used by Driver.
   515→    // Built-in packages are official cangjie libraries bundled with cjc compiler release,
   516→    // Libraries such as std module, encoding module, compress module, are built-in packages.
   517→    // Frontend knows which built-in packages the current package depends. Frontend stores
   518→    // dependent built-in packages into 'directBuiltinDependencies' or 'indirectBuiltinDependencies',
   519→    // then Driver could get these info and link dependent packages at linkage time.
   520→    std::unordered_set<std::string> directBuiltinDependencies;   /**< direct dependencies. */
   521→    std::unordered_set<std::string> indirectBuiltinDependencies; /**< indirect dependencies. */
   522→
   523→    std::vector<TempFileInfo> frontendOutputFiles; /**< .bc files to compile. */
   524→
   525→    std::vector<std::string> removedPathPrefix; /**< The removed path prefix of debug info. */
   526→
   527→    std::vector<std::string> bcInputFiles;
   528→
   529→    // Mark the input files and their input order.
   530→    std::vector<std::tuple<std::string, uint64_t>> inputFileOrder;
   531→    // Mark the input library(-l) files and their input order.
   532→    std::vector<std::tuple<std::string, uint64_t>> inputLibraryOrder;
   533→    // Mark the input link options and their input order.
   534→    std::vector<std::tuple<std::string, uint64_t>> inputLinkOptionsOrder;
   535→    // Mark the input link option and their input order.
   536→    std::vector<std::tuple<std::string, uint64_t>> inputLinkOptionOrder;
   537→
   538→    /**
   539→     * @brief Replaces an old input filename with a new one in the list.
   540→     *
   541→     * @param oldName The old filename to be replaced.
   542→     * @param newName The new filename to replace the old one.
   543→     */
   544→    void ReplaceInputFileName(const std::string& oldName, const std::string& newName)
   545→    {
   546→        for (size_t i = 0; i < inputFileOrder.size(); i++) {
   547→            std::tuple<std::string, uint64_t> oldTuple = inputFileOrder[i];
   548→            if (std::get<0>(oldTuple) == oldName) {
   549→                inputFileOrder[i] = std::make_tuple(newName, std::get<1>(oldTuple));
   550→            }
   551→        }
   552→    }

   684→    bool disableChirOpt = false;    /**< Disable Chir Optimization When use -O2 and --disable-chir-opt*/
   685→    bool disableBackendOpt = false; /**< Disable Backend Optimization When use -O2 and --disable-backend-opt*/
   686→    struct SanitizerCoverageOptions {
   687→        enum class Type {
   688→            SCK_UNKNOW = -1,
   689→            SCK_NONE = 0,
   690→            SCK_FUNCTION,
   691→            SCK_BB,
   692→        } coverageType = Type::SCK_UNKNOW;
   693→        bool traceCmp = false;
   694→        bool traceMemCmp = false;
   695→        bool tracePCGuard = false;
   696→        bool inline8bitCounters = false;
   697→        bool inlineBoolFlag = false;
   698→        bool pcTable = false;
   699→        bool stackDepth = false;
   700→
   701→        /**
   702→         * @brief Default constructor of SanitizerCoverageOptions.
   703→         *
   704→         * @return The SanitizerCoverageOptions object.
   705→         */
   706→        SanitizerCoverageOptions() = default;
   707→
   708→        /**
   709→         * @brief Sets the sanitizer coverage level.
   710→         *
   711→         * @param level The coverage level.
   712→         */
   713→        void SetSancovLevel(Type level)
   714→        {
   715→            coverageType = level;
   716→        }
   717→
   718→        /**
   719→         * @brief Checks if the sanitizer coverage feature is enabled.
   720→         *
   721→         * @return bool Returns true if the sanitizer coverage feature is enabled, otherwise returns false.
   722→         */
   723→        bool IsSancovEnabled() const
   724→        {
   725→            return traceCmp || traceMemCmp || tracePCGuard ||
   726→                inline8bitCounters || inlineBoolFlag || pcTable || stackDepth;
   727→        }
   728→
   729→        /**
   730→         * @brief Serializes the SanitizerCoverageOptions object into string.
   731→         *
   732→         * @return std::string A serialized string.
   733→         */
   734→        std::string ToSerializedString() const;
   735→    };
   736→    SanitizerCoverageOptions sancovOption;

   852→    /**
   853→     * @brief Determine if the output mode is executable.
   854→     *
   855→     * @return bool Returns true if the output mode is executable or obj and compileTarget is executable,
   856→     * otherwise returns false.
   857→     */
   858→    bool CompileExecutable() const
   859→    {
   860→        return outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::EXECUTABLE ||
   861→            (outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::OBJ && compileTarget == CompileTarget::EXECUTABLE);
   862→    }
   863→
   864→    /**
   865→     * @brief Get options backend type.
   866→     *
   867→     * @return Options::Backend The backend type.
   868→     */
   869→    Options::Backend GetOptionsBackend()
   870→    {
   871→        switch (backend) {
   872→            case Triple::BackendType::CJNATIVE:
   873→                return Options::Backend::CJNATIVE;
   874→            default:
   875→                break;
   876→        }
   877→        return Options::Backend::UNKNOWN;
   878→    }
   879→
   880→    OverflowStrategy overflowStrategy = OverflowStrategy::THROWING;
   881→

   883→     * @brief Get Cangjie library path name of host.
   884→     *
   885→     * @return std::string Cangjie library path name is a name consists of os, arch and
   886→     * backend, such as linux_aarch64_cjnative.
   887→     */
   888→    std::string GetCangjieLibHostPathName() const;

   897→    /**

   899→     *
   900→     * @return std::string The stack trace format string.

   902→    std::string GetStackTraceFormat() const
   903→    {
   904→        return "--" + StackTraceFormatToSerializedString();
   905→    };

   907→    /**
   908→     * @brief Determine if it is cross compiling.
   909→     *
   910→     * @return bool Return true If it is cross compiling.
   911→     */
   912→    inline bool IsCrossCompiling() const
   913→    {
   914→        return host != target;
   915→    }
   916→
   917→    /**
   918→     * @brief Determine if chir optimization level is over O2.
   919→     *
   920→     * @return bool Return true If chir optimization level is over O2.
   921→     */
   922→    bool IsCHIROptimizationLevelOverO2() const
   923→    {
   924→        return (!disableChirOpt) && optimizationLevel >= GlobalOptions::OptimizationLevel::O2;
   925→    }
   926→
   927→    /**
   928→     * @brief Determine if chir optimization exists.
   929→     *
   930→     * @return bool Return true If chir optimization exists.
   931→     */
   932→    bool IsOptimizationExisted(OptimizationFlag flag) const
   933→    {
   934→        if (disableChirOpt) {
   935→            return false;
   936→        }
   937→        return selectedCHIROpts.find(flag) != selectedCHIROpts.end();
   938→    }
   939→
   940→    /**
   941→     * @brief Set optimization level.
   942→     *
   943→     * @return bool Returns true If it set success.
   944→     */
   945→    bool SetOptimizationLevel(OptimizationLevel level);
   946→
   947→    /**
   948→     * @brief Checks if constant expression evaluation is enabled.
   949→     *
   950→     * @return bool Returns true if ir is enabled; otherwise returns false.
   951→     */
   952→    bool IsConstEvalEnabled() const
   953→    {
   954→        // No constant evaluation when:
   955→        // - Running with `--chir-interpreter` - everything gets interpreted anyway.
   956→        return !interpreter && !interpCHIR;
   957→    }
   958→
   959→    /**
   960→     * @brief Checks if the Sancov option is enabled.
   961→     *
   962→     * @return bool Returns true if the Sancov option is enabled, otherwise returns false.
   963→     */
   964→    bool IsSancovOptionEnabled() const
   965→    {
   966→        return sancovOption.inline8bitCounters || sancovOption.inlineBoolFlag || sancovOption.tracePCGuard ||
   967→            sancovOption.pcTable || sancovOption.stackDepth || sancovOption.traceCmp || sancovOption.traceMemCmp;
   968→    }
   969→
   970→    /**
   971→     * @brief Checks if the sanitizer is enabled.
   972→     *
   973→     * @return bool Returns true if the sanitizer is enabled; otherwise returns false.
   974→     */
   975→    inline bool EnableSanitizer() const
   976→    {
   977→        return sanitizerType != SanitizerType::NONE;
   978→    }
   979→
   980→    /**
   981→     * @brief Checks if the asan is enabled.
   982→     *
   983→     * @return bool Returns true if the asan is enabled; otherwise returns false.
   984→     */
   985→    inline bool EnableAsan() const
   986→    {
   987→        return sanitizerType == SanitizerType::ADDRESS;
   988→    }
   989→
   990→    /**
   991→     * @brief Checks if the tsan is enabled.
   992→     *
   993→     * @return bool Returns true if the tsan is enabled; otherwise returns false.
   994→     */
   995→    inline bool EnableTsan() const
   996→    {
   997→        return sanitizerType == SanitizerType::THREAD;
   998→    }
   999→
  1000→    /**

  1234→        CJC_ASSERT(index < flags.size());

  1236→    }
```

```
   354→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseFuncBody(const AST::Decl& decl)
   355→{
   356→    if (decl.astKind != AST::ASTKind::FUNC_DECL) {
   357→        return;
   358→    }
   359→    // const_cast is safe: we own the AST tree and are past the translation point for this decl.
   360→    auto& funcDecl = const_cast<AST::FuncDecl&>(static_cast<const AST::FuncDecl&>(decl));
   361→    if (funcDecl.funcBody != nullptr && funcDecl.funcBody->body != nullptr) {
   362→        funcDecl.funcBody->body.reset();
   363→    }
   364→}
   365→
   366→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseVarInitializer(AST::VarDeclAbstract& decl)
   367→{
   368→    if (decl.initializer != nullptr) {
   369→        decl.initializer.reset();
   370→    }
   371→}
   372→
   373→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies(const AST::Package& /* pkg */)
   374→{
   375→    // Release method bodies from nominal decls (class/interface/struct/enum) after batch translation.
   376→    // Uses GetMemberDecls() which is the canonical way to access members across all nominal types.
   377→    auto releaseMethodBodies = [this](const std::vector<Ptr<const AST::Decl>>& decls) {
   378→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   379→            auto& memberDecls = decl->GetMemberDecls();
   380→            for (auto& member : memberDecls) {
   381→                ReleaseFuncBody(*member);
   382→            }
   383→        }
   384→    };
   385→    releaseMethodBodies(nominalDecls);
   386→    releaseMethodBodies(genericNominalDecls);
   387→}
   388→
   389→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(const InitOrder& initOrder)
   390→{
   391→    for (auto& [file, decls] : initOrder) {
   392→        for (auto& decl : decls) {
   393→            if (auto* varDecl = DynamicCast<AST::VarDeclAbstract*>(const_cast<AST::Decl*>(decl.get()))) {
   394→                ReleaseVarInitializer(*varDecl);
   395→            }
   396→        }
   397→    }
   398→}
   399→
   400→void AST2CHIR::ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies()
   401→{
   402→    for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   403→        if (NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   404→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   405→        }
   406→    }
   407→    for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   408→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   409→    }
   410→}
   411→
   412→void AST2CHIR::TranslateAllDecls(const AST::Package& pkg, const InitOrder& initOrder)
   413→{
   414→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("AST to CHIR Translation", "TranslateAllDecls");
   415→    // step 1: translate nominal decls first (signatures only — method bodies are translated in step 3)
   416→    TranslateNominalDecls(pkg);
   417→    // NOTE: Do NOT call ReleaseTranslatedNominalBodies() here.
   418→    // TranslateNominalDecls only translates signatures (types, params, attributes).
   419→    // Method bodies are translated in step 3 via globalAndMemberFuncs, and released there
   420→    // by ReleaseFuncBody (serial) or ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies (parallel).
   421→    // Releasing here would null funcBody->body before step 3 translates it,
   422→    // causing null pointer dereference in HasDelegatedThisCall / TranslateNestedFunc.
   423→
   424→    // step 2: translate initialization of global var
   425→    TranslateInitOfGlobalVars(pkg, initOrder);
   426→    ReleaseTranslatedInitializers(initOrder);
   427→
   428→    // do this after init of gv to ensure gvinit of CustomAnnotations go after real gv's
   429→    // this is always safe because such gvinit's are generated by CHIR and cannot be referenced in source
   430→    for (auto decl : annoOnlyDecls) {
   431→        CreateAnnoOnlyDeclSig(*decl);
   432→    }
   433→
   434→    // step 3: translate body of all funcs, the process can be run in parallel according to the compilation option
   435→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   436→    if (opts.GetJobs() > 1) {
   437→        TranslateTopLevelDeclsInParallel();
   438→        ReleaseAllTranslatedFuncBodies();
   439→    } else {
   440→        for (auto decl : globalAndMemberFuncs) {
   441→            if (!NeedTranslate(*decl)) {
   442→                continue;
   443→            }
   444→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   445→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   446→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   447→            if (decl->TestAttr(AST::Attribute::GLOBAL)) {
   448→                trans.CollectValueAnnotation(*decl);
   449→            }
   450→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   451→        }
   452→        for (auto decl : std::as_const(localConstFuncs.stableOrderValue)) {
   453→            auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   454→            trans.SetTopLevel(*decl);
   455→            Translator::TranslateASTNode(*decl, trans);
   456→            ReleaseFuncBody(*decl);
   457→        }
   458→    }
   459→    // the parallel helper does not accept this type, use serialised translation
   460→    for (auto decl : annoFactoryFuncs) {
   461→        auto trans = CreateTranslator();
   462→        trans.SetTopLevel(*decl.first);
   463→        trans.TranslateAnnoFactoryFuncBody(*decl.first, *decl.second);
   464→        ReleaseFuncBody(*decl.first);
   465→    }
   466→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "TranslateOtherTopLevelDecls");
   467→
   468→    // step 4: set `CompileTimeValue` for lambda — operates on CHIR IR, unaffected by AST release
   469→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Start("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   470→    for (auto func : package->GetGlobalFuncs()) {
   471→        if (func->TestAttr(Attribute::CONST)) {
   472→            SetCompileTimeValueFlagRecursivly(*func);
   473→        }
   474→    }
   475→    Utils::ProfileRecorder::Stop("TranslateAllDecls", "SetCompileTimeValueFlag");
   476→}
```

```
   558→    }

   580→    pkgs.clear();
   581→
   582→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   583→    // Phase 3: Release managers (destruction order matters)
   584→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   585→
   586→    // 3a. TypeChecker holds TypeManager& reference, must be freed first.
   587→    delete typeChecker;

   589→

   591→    delete typeManager;
   592→    typeManager = nullptr;
   593→
   594→    // 3c. GenericInstantiationManager
   595→    delete gim;
   596→    gim = nullptr;
   597→
   598→    // 3d. TestManager holds ImportManager and TypeManager references.
   599→    delete testManager;
   600→    testManager = nullptr;
   601→
   602→    // 3e. BaseMangler — ManglerContext holds AST pointer maps.
   603→    mangler.reset();
   604→
   605→    // 3f. ImportManager — stack member, clear AST references and release imported packages.
   606→    importManager.ClearASTReferences();
   607→
   608→    // 3g. PackageManager — clear resolved dependency data.
   609→    if (packageManager) {
   610→        packageManager->ClearASTReferences();
   611→    }
   612→
   613→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   614→    // Phase 4: Release AST core data (strict order)
   615→    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
   616→
   617→    // 4a. Release AST nodes first (triggers Symbol detach).
   618→    srcPkgs.clear();
```

```
   511→void IncrementalCompilerInstance::LoadCachedCodegenResult() const

   519→
   520→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCodeGen()
   521→{
   522→    Utils::ProfileRecorder recorder("Main Stage", "CodeGen");
   523→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   524→        // Use codeGenPkgInfos if AST is released, otherwise use srcPkgs.
   525→        if (IsASTReleased()) {
   526→            for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   527→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   528→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(info.fullPackageName);
   529→            }
   530→        } else {
   531→            for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   532→                LoadCachedCodegenResult();
   533→                invocation.globalOptions.UpdateCachedDirName(srcPkg->fullPackageName);
   534→            }
   535→        }
   536→        return true;
   537→    }
   538→    // Before CodeGen, the dependency relationship of a package contains only some packages.
   539→    // So this function rearranges the dependencies of all packages.
   540→    RearrangeImportedPackageDependence();
   541→    bool ret = true;
   542→    if (IsASTReleased()) {
   543→        for (auto& info : codeGenPkgInfos) {
   544→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(info.fullPackageName, info.isEmpty, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   545→        }
   546→    } else {
   547→        for (auto& srcPkg : GetSourcePackages()) {
   548→            ret = ret && CodegenOnePackage(*srcPkg, kind == IncreKind::INCR);
   549→        }
   550→    }
   551→    return ret;
   552→}
   553→
   554→bool IncrementalCompilerInstance::PerformCjoSaving()
   555→{
   556→    if (auto& logger = IncrementalCompilationLogger::GetInstance(); logger.IsEnable()) {
   557→        std::string message;
   558→        if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE) {
   559→            message = "no change, skip cjo saving";
   560→        } else if (kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
   561→            message = "empty pkg, skip cjo saving";
   562→        } else if (invocation.globalOptions.outputMode == GlobalOptions::OutputMode::CHIR) {
   563→            message = " chir output mode, skip cjo saving";
   564→        } else {
   565→            message = "incremental cjo saving";
   566→        }
   567→        logger.LogLn(message);
   568→    }
   569→    if (kind == IncreKind::NO_CHANGE || kind == IncreKind::EMPTY_PKG) {
```
